####################################
#### Austrian economy decisions ####

AUH_decision_category_cisleithanien_industry = {

	### Decisions ###

	## Krakow Mines (3 decisions) ##

	#Clear Space for New Mines
	AUS_decision_clear_space_for_new_mines = {

		icon = GFX_decision_dynamite

		available = {
			num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 1
			AUS_ignacy_lukasiewicz = {
				is_hired_as_advisor = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = eoanb_industry_development_ongoing_flag }
		}

		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = AUS_expand_salt_and_oil_minning
		}

		cancel_trigger = {
			AUS = {
				AND = {
					NOT = { owns_state = 1321 }
					NOT = { owns_state = 88 }
				}
				NOT = {
					AUS_ignacy_lukasiewicz = {
						is_hired_as_advisor = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			civilian_factory_use = 2
		}

		fire_only_once = yes 

		days_remove = 120

		custom_cost_trigger = {
			set_temp_variable = { amount_of_money_to_check = 0.5 }
			has_specific_amount_of_money_with_inflation_included = yes
		}
		custom_cost_text = eoanb_money_cost_text
		complete_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { money_to_gain = -0.5 }
			add_money_with_tooltip_effect = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = eoanb_industry_development_ongoing_flag
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_opens_new_mines_tt
			unlock_decision_tooltip = AUS_decision_tap_into_galician_oil
			set_country_flag = AUS_oil_mines_available_flag
			set_country_flag = AUS_salt_mines_available_flag
			hidden_effect = {
				clr_country_flag = eoanb_industry_development_ongoing_flag
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 200
		}
	}

	# Tap into the Galician Oil Fields
	AUS_decision_tap_into_galician_oil = {

		icon = oil

		available = {
			num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 1
			AUS_ignacy_lukasiewicz = {
				is_hired_as_advisor = yes
			}
			has_tech = refining
			NOT = { has_country_flag = eoanb_industry_development_ongoing_flag }
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = AUS_oil_mines_available_flag
			has_completed_focus = AUS_expand_salt_and_oil_minning
		}

		cancel_trigger = {

				}
				NOT = {
						AUS_ignacy_lukasiewicz = {
						is_hired_as_advisor = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			civilian_factory_use = 2
		}

		fire_only_once = yes
		days_remove = 120

		custom_cost_trigger = {
			set_temp_variable = { amount_of_money_to_check = 0.25 }
			has_specific_amount_of_money_with_inflation_included = yes
		}
		custom_cost_text = eoanb_money_cost_text

			}
		}

			}

	# Clear Space for New Factories in the Periphery Regions
	AUS_decison_clear_space_for_new_factories_periphery_regions = { 
	
		available = {
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = AUS_periphery_region_investment_count
				value < 2
			}
		}

		state_target = yes
		on_map_mode = map_only

		targets = {1321 88 91 89 80 1055 970 }

		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = AUS_support_local_industry_and_development_banks
		}

		days_remove = 40
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			set_temp_variable = { amount_of_money_to_check = 0.15 }
			has_specific_amount_of_money_with_inflation_included = yes
		}
		custom_cost_text = eoanb_money_cost_text
		complete_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { money_to_gain = -0.15 }
			add_money_with_tooltip_effect = yes
			modify_country_flag = {
				flag = AUS_periphery_region_investment_count
				value = 1
			}
		}

		icon = infrastructure

		allowed = { 
			tag = AUS
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		ai_will_do ={
			base = 100
		}

		remove_effect = {
			FROM = {
				set_state_flag = AUH_periphery_region_cleared
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = AUH_periphery_clear_tt
			unlock_decision_tooltip = AUS_decison_build_new_factories_in_the_periphery_regions
			modify_country_flag = {
				flag = AUS_periphery_region_investment_count
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}

	# Build New Factories in the Periphery Regions

	#Open Coal Mines in Brüx
	AUS_decision_open_coal_mines_in_brux = {

		icon = GFX_decision_dynamite

		available = {
			num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 1
			NOT = { has_country_flag = eoanb_industry_development_ongoing_flag }
		}

		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = AUS_brux_coal_excavation
		}

		modifier = {
			civilian_factory_use = 2
		}

		fire_only_once = yes
		days_remove = 120

		custom_cost_trigger = {
			set_temp_variable = { amount_of_money_to_check = 0.25 }
			has_specific_amount_of_money_with_inflation_included = yes
		}
		custom_cost_text = eoanb_money_cost_text
		complete_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { money_to_gain = -0.25 }
			add_money_with_tooltip_effect = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = eoanb_industry_development_ongoing_flag
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_tech = refining
				}
				69 = {
					add_building_construction = {
						type = coal_mine
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_resource = {
					type = coal
					amount = 4
					state = 69
				}
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				bonus = 0.35
				uses = 2
				category = resource_extraction_tech
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				clr_country_flag = eoanb_industry_development_ongoing_flag
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 200
		}
	}

	# Pay Out The Jewish Victims
	AUS_decision_pay_out_the_jewish_victims = {

		icon = GFX_decision_judaism
		
		#allowed = { tag = AUS }

		available = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = eoanb_industry_development_ongoing_flag }
		}

		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = AUS_do_something_about_the_economic_boycotts
			if =  {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = AUS_try_to_calm_down_the_polish_peasants
				}

				has_completed_focus = AUS_ban_the_extremists
			}
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		custom_cost_trigger = {
			set_temp_variable = {
				amount_of_money_to_check = 1
			}
			has_specific_amount_of_money_with_inflation_included = yes
		}
		custom_cost_text = eoanb_money_cost_text

		days_remove = 50

		complete_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { money_to_gain = -1 }
			add_money_with_inflation_included_with_tooltip_effect = yes
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = {
				unemployment_value = -0.0001
			}
			add_unemployment_effect = yes
			increase_ps_by_one = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_disable_resistance_in_galicia_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				88 = {
					force_disable_resistance = AUS
				}
				1321 = {
					force_disable_resistance = AUS
				}
			}
			EOANBSYS_institutions_innovative_add_one = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				clr_country_flag = eoanb_industry_development_ongoing_flag
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 100
		}

		icon = generic_factory
		allowed = { always = no }
		available = {
			owns_state = 1321
			1321 = {
				industrial_complex > 1
			}
		}
		activation = { always = no }
		priority = 50
		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = 1321
			}
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		is_good = yes
		days_mission_timeout = 1600
		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = no
				}
				add_political_power = -50
				add_stability = -0.04
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			1321 = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
			}
			add_stability = 0.02
			set_temp_variable = {
				unemployment_value = -0.0002
			}
			add_unemployment_effect = yes
			set_temp_variable = {
				eoanb_prestige_change = 3
			}
			eoanb_change_prestige_score = yes
			EOANBSYS_institutions_innovative_add_one = yes
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 100
		}
	}

		}

		}
		custom_cost_text = eoanb_money_cost_text

			set_temp_variable = { money_to_gain = -0.15 }

				flag = AUS_minority_region_investment_count

			}

		}

				value = -1

					}
				}

					limit = {
						AUS = {
							has_idea = AUH_idea_founded_new_universities
						}

						idea = AUH_idea_founded_new_universities

					}

						25 = {
							add_tech_bonus = {
								bonus = 0.25

								category = humanities_tech
							}
						}
						25 = {
							add_tech_bonus = {
								bonus = 0.25
								uses = 1
								category = art_tech
							}
						}
						25 = {
							add_tech_bonus = {
								bonus = 0.25
								uses = 1
								category = chemistry_tech
							}
						}
						25 = {
							add_tech_bonus = {
								bonus = 0.25
								uses = 1
								category = biochemistry_tech
							}
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					AUS = {
						add_timed_idea = {
							idea = AUH_idea_founded_new_universities
							days = 180
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					HUN = {
						owns_state = FROM
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						HUN = {
							has_idea = AUH_idea_founded_new_universities
						}
					}
					modify_timed_idea = {
						idea = AUH_idea_founded_new_universities
						days = 60
					}
					random_list = {
						25 = {
							add_tech_bonus = {
								bonus = 0.25

								}
							}
						25 = {
							add_tech_bonus = {
								bonus = 0.25

							}
						}
						25 = {

								bonus = 0.25

							}
						}
						25 = {
						add_tech_bonus = {
								bonus = 0.25

							}
						}
					}
				}
				else = {

	# Give government fundings for the Polish industry
	AUS_decision_give_government_fundings_for_the_polsih_industry = {

		icon = GFX_decision_money

		available = {
			num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 0
			NOT = { has_country_flag = eoanb_industry_development_ongoing_flag }
		}

		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = AUS_help_them_up_from_poverty
			89 = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = dynmod_AUS_galician_poverty }
			}
			88 = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = dynmod_AUS_galician_poverty }
			}
			91 = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = dynmod_AUS_galician_poverty }
			}
			1321 = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = dynmod_AUS_galician_poverty }
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			civilian_factory_use = 1
		}

		fire_only_once = yes 

		days_remove = 80

		custom_cost_trigger = {
			set_temp_variable = { amount_of_money_to_check = 0.5 }
		}
		custom_cost_text = eoanb_money_cost_text
		complete_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { money_to_gain = -0.5 }
			add_money_with_tooltip_effect = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = eoanb_industry_development_ongoing_flag
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = {
				unemployment_value = -0.0005
			}
			add_unemployment_effect = yes
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					1321 = {
						add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
					}
				}
				25 = {
					88 = {
						add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
					}
				}
				25 = {
					91 = {
						add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
					}
				}
				25 = {
					89 = {
						add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_reduce_polish_poverty_tt
			add_to_variable = {AUS_gal_pov_lm = 0.03 tooltip = local_manpower_tooltip }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = AUS_gal_pov_lm
				min = 0
				max = 1
			}
			add_to_variable = {AUS_gal_pov_ls = 0.08 tooltip = local_supplies_tooltip }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = AUS_gal_pov_ls
				min = 0
				max = 1
			}
			add_to_variable = {AUS_gal_pov_srf = 0.04 tooltip = state_resources_factor_tooltip }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = AUS_gal_pov_srf
				min = 0
				max = 1
			}
			add_to_variable = {AUS_gal_pov_psbf = 0.04 tooltip = production_speed_buildings_factor_tooltip }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = AUS_gal_pov_psbf 
				min = 0
				max = 1
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						check_variable = {
							var = AUS_gal_pov_lm
							value = 0
							compare = greater_than_or_equals
						}
						check_variable = {
							var = AUS_gal_pov_ls 
							value = 0
							compare = greater_than_or_equals
						}
						check_variable = {
							var = AUS_gal_pov_srf
							value = 0
							compare = greater_than_or_equals
						}
						check_variable = {
							var = AUS_gal_pov_psbf
							value = 0
							compare = greater_than_or_equals
						}
					}
				}

				88 = { remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = dynmod_AUS_galician_poverty } }
				89 = { remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = dynmod_AUS_galician_poverty } }
				91 = { remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = dynmod_AUS_galician_poverty } }
				1321 = { remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = dynmod_AUS_galician_poverty } }
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				clr_country_flag = eoanb_industry_development_ongoing_flag
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 200
		}
	}

	# The Issue Of Semi-Trialism
	AUS_mission_the_issue_of_semi_trialism = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_monarchy
		allowed = { always = no }
		activation = { always = no }
		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = AUS_voting_mission_tt
			}
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = no
			}
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_completed_focus = AUS_the_deadlock_got_us
					}
				}

				check_variable = {
					var = CZE_REVOLT_RISK
					value = 0.50
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
					tooltip = AUS_czech_uproar_bigger_than_fifty_percent_tt
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = AUS_still_try_to_push_on_with_the_law
				}

				check_variable = {
					var = AUS_proposal_support
					value = 0.05
					compare = less_than_or_equals
					tooltip = AUS_less_than_five_percent_support_tt
				}
			}
		}
		priority = 100
		is_good = yes
		days_mission_timeout = 120
		timeout_effect = {
			set_country_flag = AUS_the_issue_of_semi_trialism_finished
			AUS_decide_parliament_votes = yes
			clear_variable = AUS_bribe_reveal_chance
		}
		cancel_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = AUS_the_issue_of_semi_trialism_finished
				AUS_decide_parliament_votes = yes
				clear_variable = AUS_bribe_reveal_chance
				country_event = { id = austria_hungary.306 days = 5 }
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 100
		}
	}

	### General Decisions ###

	# Meet with the Liberal representatives
	AUS_meet_with_the_liberal_representatives = { 

		icon = GFX_decision_envelope

		available = { 
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = AUS_reichsrat_decision_ongoing_tt
				NOT = { has_country_flag = AUS_reichsrat_decision_ongoing }
			}
		}

		visible = {
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_active_mission = AUS_mission_semi_trialism_for_bohemia
					has_active_mission = AUS_mission_the_issue_of_semi_trialism
					has_active_mission = AUS_mission_budget_law
					has_active_mission = AUS_mission_minor_compromise_hohenwart
					has_active_mission = AUS_mission_full_compromise_with_the_czechs
					has_active_mission = AUS_mission_vote_on_the_status_of_the_bohemian_crownland
				}
				OR = {
					has_country_leader = {
						character = AUS_alfred_jozef_potocki
						ruling_only = yes
					}
					has_country_leader = {
						character = AUS_karl_sigmund_von_hohenwart
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}

		cost = 30
		days_remove = AUS_reichsrat_days_remove_1 #25
		days_re_enable = AUS_reichsrat_days_re_enable_1 #20

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = AUS_reichsrat_decision_ongoing
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = AUS_reichsrat_decision_ongoing
			custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_give_support_between_five_and_eight_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				set_temp_variable_to_random = {
					var = AUS_random_support
					min = 0.05
					max = 0.08
				}

	# Bribe some of the representatives
	AUS_bribe_some_of_the_representatives = {
		
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_welfare
		
		available = {

				tooltip = AUS_reichsrat_decision_ongoing_tt
				NOT = { has_country_flag = AUS_reichsrat_decision_ongoing }
			}
		}

				has_active_mission = AUS_mission_the_big_day
				has_active_mission = AUS_mission_semi_trialism_for_bohemia
				has_active_mission = AUS_mission_the_issue_of_semi_trialism
				has_active_mission = AUS_mission_reforming_the_court_system
				has_active_mission = AUS_mission_election_reform_auersperg
				has_active_mission = AUS_mission_reverse_the_may_laws
				has_active_mission = AUS_mission_reichsvolksschulgesetz
				has_active_mission = AUS_mission_moderate_may_laws
				has_active_mission = AUS_mission_budget_law
				has_active_mission = AUS_mission_minor_compromise_hohenwart
				has_active_mission = AUS_mission_full_compromise_with_the_czechs
				has_active_mission = AUS_mission_trade_code_ammendment
				has_active_mission = AUS_mission_health_insurance_law
				has_active_mission = AUS_mission_accident_insurance_act
				has_active_mission = AUS_mission_first_election_reform_taaffe
				has_active_mission = AUS_mission_second_election_reform_taaffe
				has_active_mission = AUS_mission_vote_on_the_status_of_the_bohemian_crownland
				has_active_mission = AUS_mission_the_may_laws
			}
		}

		custom_cost_trigger = {
			set_temp_variable = { amount_of_money_to_check = 1.5 }
		}
		custom_cost_text = eoanb_money_cost_text
		days_remove = 5
		days_re_enable = 20

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = AUS_reichsrat_decision_ongoing
			set_temp_variable = { money_to_gain = -1.5 }
			add_money_with_tooltip_effect = yes
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = AUS_idea_minor_corruption
				days = 80
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = AUS_reichsrat_decision_ongoing
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_active_mission = AUS_mission_karl_von_auersperg
				}
				add_days_mission_timeout = {
					mission = AUS_mission_karl_von_auersperg
					days = -20
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_active_mission = AUS_mission_eduard_von_taaffe
				}
				add_days_mission_timeout = {
					mission = AUS_mission_eduard_von_taaffe
					days = -20
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_active_mission = AUS_mission_the_two_hard_liners
				}
				add_days_mission_timeout = {
					mission = AUS_mission_the_two_hard_liners
					days = -20
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_active_mission = AUS_mission_alfred_jozef_potocki
				}
				add_days_mission_timeout = {
					mission = AUS_mission_alfred_jozef_potocki
					days = -20
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_active_mission = AUS_mission_karl_sigmund_von_hohenwart
				}
				add_days_mission_timeout = {
					mission = AUS_mission_karl_sigmund_von_hohenwart
					days = -20
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_active_mission = AUS_mission_adolf_von_auersperg
				}
				add_days_mission_timeout = {
					mission = AUS_mission_adolf_von_auersperg
					days = -20
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_active_mission = AUS_mission_eduard_von_taaffe_second_term
				}
				add_days_mission_timeout = {
					mission = AUS_mission_eduard_von_taaffe_second_term
					days = -20
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_give_support_between_five_and_eight_tt
			custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_increase_bribe_chance_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				set_temp_variable_to_random = {
					var = AUS_random_support
					min = 0.05
					max = 0.08
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = AUS_proposal_support
					value = AUS_random_support
				}
				clamp_variable = {
					var = AUS_proposal_support
					min = 0
					max = 1
				}

				add_to_variable = {
					var = AUS_bribe_reveal_chance
					value = 0.03
				}
				clamp_variable = {
					var = AUS_bribe_reveal_chance
					min = 0
					max = 1
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = AUS_bribe_reveal_chance
				
				custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_take_support_ten_tt
				hidden_effect = {
					add_to_variable = {
						var = AUS_proposal_support
						value = -0.10
					}
					clamp_variable = {
						var = AUS_proposal_support
						min = 0
						max = 1
					}
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = AUS_idea_minor_corruption
					add_idea = AUS_idea_major_corruption_scandal
				}
			}
		}

		ai_will_do ={
			base = 50
		}
	}

AUH_decision_category_panic_of_1873 = {

	# Panic Of 1873
	AUS_mission_panic_of_1873 = {
		icon = generic_factory
		allowed = { always = no }
		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = dynmod_AUS_panic_of_1873 }
			}
		}
		activation = { always = no }
		priority = 50
		fire_only_once = yes
		is_good = yes
		days_mission_timeout = 365

		complete_effect = {
			add_stability = 0.20
			add_war_support = 0.05
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = dynmod_AUS_panic_of_1873 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_leader = {
						character = AUS_adolf_von_auersperg
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
				add_days_mission_timeout = {
					mission = AUS_mission_adolf_von_auersperg
					days = 50
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_leader = {
						character = AUS_eduard_von_taaffe
						ruling_only = yes
					}
					has_active_mission = AUS_mission_eduard_von_taaffe_second_term
				}
				add_days_mission_timeout = {
					mission = AUS_mission_eduard_von_taaffe_second_term
					days = 50
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_leader = {
						character = AUS_karl_sigmund_von_hohenwart
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
				add_days_mission_timeout = {
					mission = AUS_mission_karl_sigmund_von_hohenwart
					days = 50
				}
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = AUS_idea_the_economy_rises_like_a_phoenix
				years = 15
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = AUS_idea_the_banks_are_on_our_side }
				remove_ideas = {
					AUS_idea_the_banks_are_on_our_side
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = AUS_idea_expoliting_the_helping_hands }
				remove_ideas = {
					AUS_idea_expoliting_the_helping_hands
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = AUS_work_with_the_bankers
				}
				activate_mission = AUS_mission_the_banks_want_their_money
				unlock_decision_tooltip = AUS_decision_repay_the_banks
			}
		}
		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_leader = {
						character = AUS_adolf_von_auersperg
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
				add_days_mission_timeout = {
					mission = AUS_mission_adolf_von_auersperg
					days = -80
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_leader = {
						character = AUS_eduard_von_taaffe
						ruling_only = yes
					}
					has_active_mission = AUS_mission_eduard_von_taaffe_second_term
				}
				add_days_mission_timeout = {
					mission = AUS_mission_eduard_von_taaffe_second_term
					days = -80
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_leader = {
						character = AUS_karl_sigmund_von_hohenwart
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
				add_days_mission_timeout = {
					mission = AUS_mission_karl_sigmund_von_hohenwart
					days = -80
				}
			}
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = dynmod_AUS_panic_of_1873 }
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = AUS_idea_mismanagement_of_the_crisis
				years = 10
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = AUS_idea_the_banks_are_on_our_side }
				remove_ideas = {
					AUS_idea_the_banks_are_on_our_side
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = AUS_idea_expoliting_the_helping_hands }
				remove_ideas = {
					AUS_idea_expoliting_the_helping_hands
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = AUS_work_with_the_bankers
				}
				activate_mission = AUS_mission_the_banks_want_their_money
				unlock_decision_tooltip = AUS_decision_repay_the_banks
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 100
		}
	}

###########################
#### Election Campaign ####
###########################

AUH_decision_election_campaign = { 
	### Normal Mission ###
	AUS_mission_hohenwart_election = {
		icon = generic_factory
		allowed = { always = no }
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = no
			}
		}
		activation = { always = no }
		priority = 1000
		fire_only_once = yes
		is_good = yes
		days_mission_timeout = 100
		timeout_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_result_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							var = AUS_election_conservative_support_var
							value = 0.50
							compare = greater_than_or_equals
						}
					}

					complete_national_focus = AUS_a_federalist_majority
				}
				else = {
					complete_national_focus = AUS_a_federalist_minority
				}
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 100
		}
	}
	### Missions for the AI ###
	AUS_mission_expand_influence_in_south_bukovina = {

		icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = { state = 1055 } 
		}

		on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view

		fire_only_once = no

		days_mission_timeout = 3

		is_good = no

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		activation = {
			always = no
		}

		visible = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_completed_focus = AUS_dissolve_the_parliament
					NOT = { 
						OR = {
							has_completed_focus = AUS_a_federalist_majority
							has_completed_focus = AUS_a_federalist_minority
						}
					}
				}
				
			}
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						1055 = {
							has_state_flag = AUS_election_small_region 
							has_state_flag = AUS_election_medium_region	
						}
					}
				}

				if = {
					limit = { 1055 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 3 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_one_liberal_support
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 1055 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 2 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_one_liberal_support
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 1055 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 1 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_one_liberal_support
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { 
					1055 = { has_state_flag = AUS_election_large_region }
				}

				if = {
					limit = { 1055 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 3 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_two_liberal_support
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 1055 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 2 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_one_liberal_support
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 1055 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 1 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_one_liberal_support
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { 
					1055 = { has_state_flag = AUS_election_very_large_region }
				}

				if = {
					limit = { 1055 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 3 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_two_liberal_support
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 1055 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 2 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_two_liberal_support
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 1055 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 1 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_one_liberal_support
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = { 1055 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 3 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_four_liberal_support
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 1055 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 2 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_four_liberal_support
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 1055 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 1 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_three_liberal_support
				}
			}
			1055 = {
				set_state_flag = { flag = AUS_ai_recently_expanded_influence_election_flag value = 1 days = 10 }
			}
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = austria_hungary.961 days = 1 random_days = 4 } }
			### Small ###
			if = {
				limit = {
					1055 = {
						has_state_flag = AUS_election_small_region
						has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 3 }
					}
				}

				AUS =  {
					subtract_from_variable = {
						var = AUS_election_conservative_support_var
						value = 0.01
					}
					add_to_variable = {
						var = AUS_election_liberal_support_var
						value = 0.01
					}
				}
				1055 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								has_state_flag = {
									flag = AUS_election_influence_control_conservatives
									value = 1
								}
							}
						}
						modify_state_flag = {
							flag = AUS_election_influence_control_conservatives
							value = -1
						}
					}
					modify_state_flag = {
						flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals
						value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					1055 = {
						has_state_flag = AUS_election_small_region
						has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 2 }
					}
				}
				AUS =  {
					subtract_from_variable = {
						var = AUS_election_conservative_support_var
						value = 0.01
					}
					add_to_variable = {
						var = AUS_election_liberal_support_var
						value = 0.01
					}
				}
				1055 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								has_state_flag = {
									flag = AUS_election_influence_control_conservatives
									value = 1
								}
							}
						}
						modify_state_flag = {
							flag = AUS_election_influence_control_conservatives
							value = -1
						}
					}
					modify_state_flag = {
						flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals
						value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					1055 = {
						has_state_flag = AUS_election_small_region
						has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 1 }
					}
				}

		icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}

			highlight_state_targets = { state = 80 } 
		}

		on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view

		fire_only_once = no

		days_mission_timeout = 3

		is_good = no

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		activation = {
			always = no
		}

		visible = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_completed_focus = AUS_dissolve_the_parliament
					NOT = { 
						OR = {
							has_completed_focus = AUS_a_federalist_majority
							has_completed_focus = AUS_a_federalist_minority
						}
					}
				}
				
			}
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						80 = {
							has_state_flag = AUS_election_small_region 
							has_state_flag = AUS_election_medium_region	
						}
					}
				}

				if = {
					limit = { 80 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 3 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_one_liberal_support
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 80 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 2 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_one_liberal_support
				}

					limit = { 80 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 1 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_one_liberal_support
				}

					80 = { has_state_flag = AUS_election_large_region }

		icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}

			highlight_state_targets = { state = 1321 } 
		}

		on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view

		fire_only_once = no

		days_mission_timeout = 10

		is_good = no

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		activation = {
			always = no
		}

		visible = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_completed_focus = AUS_dissolve_the_parliament
					NOT = { 
						OR = {
							has_completed_focus = AUS_a_federalist_majority
							has_completed_focus = AUS_a_federalist_minority
						}
					}
				}
				
			}
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						1321 = {
							has_state_flag = AUS_election_small_region 
							has_state_flag = AUS_election_medium_region	
						}
					}
				}

				if = {
					limit = { 1321 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 3 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_one_liberal_support
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 1321 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 2 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_one_liberal_support
				}

	AUS_mission_expand_influence_in_olsa_silesia = {

		icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = { state = 72 } 
		}

		on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view

		fire_only_once = no

		days_mission_timeout = 3

		is_good = no

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		activation = {
			always = no
		}

		visible = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_completed_focus = AUS_dissolve_the_parliament
					NOT = { 
						OR = {
							has_completed_focus = AUS_a_federalist_majority
							has_completed_focus = AUS_a_federalist_minority
						}
					}
				}
				
			}
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						72 = {
							has_state_flag = AUS_election_small_region 
							has_state_flag = AUS_election_medium_region	
						}
					}
				}

				if = {
					limit = { 72 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 3 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_one_liberal_support
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 72 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 2 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_one_liberal_support
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 72 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 1 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_one_liberal_support
				}
			}

				limit = { 
					72 = { has_state_flag = AUS_election_large_region }
				}

					limit = { 72 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 3 } } }

				}

		is_good = no

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		activation = {
			always = no
		}

		visible = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_completed_focus = AUS_dissolve_the_parliament
					NOT = { 
						OR = {
							has_completed_focus = AUS_a_federalist_majority
							has_completed_focus = AUS_a_federalist_minority
						}
					}
				}
				
			}
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						75 = {
							has_state_flag = AUS_election_small_region 
							has_state_flag = AUS_election_medium_region	
						}
					}
				}

				if = {
					limit = { 75 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 3 } } }

				}

					limit = { 75 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 2 } } }

				}

	AUS_mission_expand_influence_in_upper_austria = {

		icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = { state = 152 } 
		}

		on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view

		fire_only_once = no

		days_mission_timeout = 8

		is_good = no

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		activation = {
			always = no
		}

		visible = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_completed_focus = AUS_dissolve_the_parliament
					NOT = { 
						OR = {
							has_completed_focus = AUS_a_federalist_majority
							has_completed_focus = AUS_a_federalist_minority
						}
					}
				}
				
			}
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						152 = {
							has_state_flag = AUS_election_small_region 
							has_state_flag = AUS_election_medium_region	
						}
					}
				}

				if = {
					limit = { 152 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 3 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_one_liberal_support
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 152 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 2 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_one_liberal_support
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 152 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 1 } } }

					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_two_liberal_support
				}

	AUS_mission_expand_influence_in_lower_austria = {

		icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = { state = 4 } 
		}

		on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view

		fire_only_once = no

		days_mission_timeout = 10

		is_good = no

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		activation = {
			always = no
		}

		visible = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_completed_focus = AUS_dissolve_the_parliament
					NOT = { 
						OR = {
							has_completed_focus = AUS_a_federalist_majority
							has_completed_focus = AUS_a_federalist_minority
						}
					}
				}
				
			}
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						4 = {
							has_state_flag = AUS_election_small_region 
							has_state_flag = AUS_election_medium_region	
						}
					}
				}

				if = {
					limit = { 4 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 3 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_one_liberal_support
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 4 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 2 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_one_liberal_support
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 4 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 1 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_one_liberal_support
				}
			}

				limit = { 
					4 = { has_state_flag = AUS_election_large_region }
				}

					limit = { 4 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 3 } } }

				}
				if = {
					limit = { 4 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 1 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_one_liberal_support
				}

		activation = {

					}
				}
				
			}
		}

	AUS_mission_expand_influence_in_trieste = {

		icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}

			highlight_state_targets = { state = 1235 } 
		}

		on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view

		fire_only_once = no

		days_mission_timeout = 8

		is_good = no

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		activation = {
			always = no
		}

		visible = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_completed_focus = AUS_dissolve_the_parliament
					NOT = { 
						OR = {
							has_completed_focus = AUS_a_federalist_majority
							has_completed_focus = AUS_a_federalist_minority
						}
					}
				}
				
			}
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						1235 = {
							has_state_flag = AUS_election_small_region 
							has_state_flag = AUS_election_medium_region	
						}
					}
				}

				if = {
					limit = { 1235 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 3 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_one_liberal_support
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 1235 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 2 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_one_liberal_support
				}

	AUS_mission_expand_influence_in_istria = {

		icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = { state = 1236 } 
		}

		on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view

		fire_only_once = no

		days_mission_timeout = 5

		is_good = no

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		activation = {
			always = no
		}

		visible = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_completed_focus = AUS_dissolve_the_parliament
					NOT = { 
						OR = {
							has_completed_focus = AUS_a_federalist_majority
							has_completed_focus = AUS_a_federalist_minority
						}
					}
				}
				
			}
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						1236 = {
							has_state_flag = AUS_election_small_region 
							has_state_flag = AUS_election_medium_region	
						}
					}
				}

				if = {
					limit = { 1236 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 3 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_one_liberal_support
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 1236 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 2 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_one_liberal_support
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 1236 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 1 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_one_liberal_support
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { 
					1236 = { has_state_flag = AUS_election_large_region }
				}

				if = {
					limit = { 1236 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 3 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_two_liberal_support

				if = {
					limit = { 1236 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 2 } } }

				}
				if = {
					limit = { 1236 = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals value = 1 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_one_liberal_support
				}
			}

					1236 = { has_state_flag = AUS_election_very_large_region }

				}

					}
				}
				
			}
		}

					}
				}

		activation = {

		}

							has_completed_focus = AUS_a_federalist_minority
						}
					}
				}
				
			}
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {

							has_state_flag = AUS_election_medium_region

					}
				}

				if = {

	### Player Decisions ###
	AUS_decision_small_states_expand_election_influence = {

		icon = {
			key = GFX_AUH_decision_election_control_none
			trigger = {
				FROM = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_conservatives value = 1 } } 
			}
		}
		icon = {
			key = GFX_AUH_decision_election_control_weak
			trigger = {
				FROM = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_conservatives value = 2 } }
			}
		}
		icon = {
			key = GFX_AUH_decision_election_control_strong
			trigger = {
				FROM = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_conservatives value = 3 } }
			}
		}
		icon = {
			key = GFX_AUH_decision_election_control_total
			trigger = {
				FROM = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_conservatives value = 4 } }
			}
		}

		available = {
			has_full_control_of_state = FROM
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = AUS_already_expanding_influence_flag
			}
			hidden_trigger = {
				NOT = { FROM = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_conservatives value = 4 } } }
			}
		}

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = { state = FROM } 
		}

		on_map_mode = map_only
		cost = 5
		state_target = yes
		fire_only_once = no
		days_remove = 3
		targets = { 1055 80 72 74 69 1010 39 1234 736 103 970 1203 }

		visible = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_completed_focus = AUS_dissolve_the_parliament
					NOT = { 
						OR = {
							has_completed_focus = AUS_a_federalist_majority
							has_completed_focus = AUS_a_federalist_minority
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = AUS_already_expanding_influence_flag
		}

		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						FROM = { has_state_flag = AUS_election_small_region }
						FROM = { has_state_flag = AUS_election_medium_region }
					}
				}

				if = {
					limit = { FROM = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_conservatives value = 3 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_one_conservative_support
				}
				if = {
					limit = { FROM = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_conservatives value = 2 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_one_conservative_support
				}
				if = {
					limit = { FROM = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_conservatives value = 1 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_one_conservative_support
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { 
					FROM = { has_state_flag = AUS_election_large_region }
				}

				if = {
					limit = { FROM = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_conservatives value = 3 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_two_conservative_support
				}
				if = {
					limit = { FROM = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_conservatives value = 2 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_one_conservative_support
				}
				if = {
					limit = { FROM = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_conservatives value = 1 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_one_conservative_support
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { 
					FROM = { has_state_flag = AUS_election_very_large_region }
				}

				if = {
					limit = { FROM = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_conservatives value = 3 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_two_conservative_support
				}
				if = {
					limit = { FROM = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_conservatives value = 2 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_two_conservative_support
				}
				if = {
					limit = { FROM = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_conservatives value = 1 } } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = AUS_election_give_one_conservative_support

						modify_state_flag = {
							flag = AUS_election_influence_control_conservatives
							value = 1
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = {
									has_state_flag = {
										flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals
										value = 1
									}
								}
							}
							modify_state_flag = {
								flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals
								value = -1
							}
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							has_state_flag = AUS_election_very_large_region
							has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_conservatives value = 1 }
						}
					}
					AUS =  {
						add_to_variable = {
							var = AUS_election_conservative_support_var
							value = 0.01
						}
						subtract_from_variable = {
							var = AUS_election_liberal_support_var
							value = 0.01
						}
					}
					FROM = {
						modify_state_flag = {
							flag = AUS_election_influence_control_conservatives
							value = 1
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = {
									has_state_flag = {
										flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals
										value = 1
									}
								}
							}
							modify_state_flag = {
								flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals
								value = -1
							}
						}
					}
				}

				### Metropolis ###
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							has_state_flag = AUS_election_metropolis
							has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_conservatives value = 3 }
						}
					}

					AUS =  {
						add_to_variable = {
							var = AUS_election_conservative_support_var
							value = 0.04
						}
						subtract_from_variable = {
							var = AUS_election_liberal_support_var
							value = 0.04
						}
					}
					FROM = {
						modify_state_flag = {
							flag = AUS_election_influence_control_conservatives
							value = 1
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = {
									has_state_flag = {
										flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals
										value = 1
									}
								}
							}
							modify_state_flag = {
								flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals
								value = -1
							}
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							has_state_flag = AUS_election_metropolis
							has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_conservatives value = 2 }
						}
					}
					AUS =  {
						add_to_variable = {
							var = AUS_election_conservative_support_var
							value = 0.04
						}
						subtract_from_variable = {
							var = AUS_election_liberal_support_var
							value = 0.04
						}
					}
					FROM = {
						modify_state_flag = {
							flag = AUS_election_influence_control_conservatives
							value = 1
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = {
									has_state_flag = {
										flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals
										value = 1
									}
								}
							}
							modify_state_flag = {
								flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals
								value = -1
							}
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							has_state_flag = AUS_election_metropolis
							has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_conservatives value = 1 }
						}
					}
					AUS =  {
						add_to_variable = {
							var = AUS_election_conservative_support_var
							value = 0.03
						}
						subtract_from_variable = {
							var = AUS_election_liberal_support_var
							value = 0.03
						}
					}
					FROM = {
						modify_state_flag = {
							flag = AUS_election_influence_control_conservatives
							value = 1
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = {
									has_state_flag = {
										flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals
										value = 1
									}
								}
							}
							modify_state_flag = {
								flag = AUS_election_influence_control_liberals
								value = -1
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 30
				NOT = { FROM = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_conservatives value = 4 } } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = { has_state_flag = { flag = AUS_election_influence_control_conservatives value = 4 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				FROM = { has_state_flag = AUS_ai_recently_expanded_influence_election_flag }
			}
		}
	}
}
